--------------------------------------------------------------
      SR1 = Ratio of Applied stress/Yield Stress (?<? 1.0)
      SR2 = Global Interaction Ratio: Applied Stress/Critical Stress (?<? 1.0)

      For Yielding (Global stresses(Sx,Sy) are combined with the stress induced by the stiff bending)
      For Buckling (Global stresses(Sx,Sy) are considered alone)
